
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Analyze the geometric properties and relative positioning of the torus and sphere to identify the tangent circles formed in each orientation.'}, {'objective': 'Derive expressions for the radii of the tangent circles when the torus rests externally tangent to the sphere in the two different orientations.'}, {'objective': 'Calculate the difference between the two tangent circle radii and simplify it to a fraction in lowest terms.'}, {'objective': 'Find and return the sum of the numerator and denominator of the simplified fraction as the final answer.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- A torus T is generated by revolving a circle of radius 3 around an axis in the plane of the circle, with the axis located 6 units from the circle's center. This creates a standard torus (donut shape) with a major radius R = 6 and minor radius r = 3.
- A sphere S has radius 11.
- The torus T is placed externally tangent to the sphere S in two distinct configurations, each time tangent along a circle.
- In one configuration, the circle of tangency on the torus has radius r_i.
- In the other configuration, the circle of tangency on the torus has radius r_o.
- The problem involves finding the difference r_i - r_o expressed as a reduced fraction m/n, then summing m + n.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The torus is defined by two radii: the major radius (distance from the center of the tube to the axis of revolution) and the minor radius (radius of the tube).
- The sphere and torus are externally tangent, meaning they touch but do not intersect, and the point(s) of contact form a circle on the torus.
- The two tangent circles correspond to two different positions or orientations of the torus relative to the sphere.
- The radii r_i and r_o represent the radii of these tangent circles on the torus surface.
- The difference r_i - r_o is a key quantity, likely related to the geometry of the torus and sphere and their relative positions.
- The tangency condition imposes geometric constraints linking the torus parameters and the sphere radius.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in geometry, specifically 3D geometry involving surfaces of revolution.
- Concepts involved include the geometry of tori and spheres, external tangency, and circle radii on curved surfaces.
- Subfields include differential geometry (surface properties), and possibly algebraic geometry if equations of surfaces are used.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and advanced geometry contexts.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The problem states "when T rests on the outside of S" twice, which may be a typographical error; likely one should be "inside" or a different configuration.
- The exact positions or orientations of the torus relative to the sphere in each tangent case are not explicitly described.
- The nature of the tangent circles (their location on the torus) is not detailed.
- Potential complexity arises in determining the exact geometric relationships and computing the radii without explicit coordinate systems or equations.
- Multiple configurations might exist, requiring careful interpretation of the problem's intended meaning.

The torus is generated by revolving a circle of radius r = 3 around an axis in the plane of the circle, with the axis located a distance R = 6 from the circle's center. The standard implicit equation of such a torus centered at the origin with the axis of revolution along the z-axis is:\n\n((sqrt(x^2 + y^2) - R)^2 + z^2) = r^2\n\nMore explicitly, the implicit equation of the torus is:\n\n(x^2 + y^2 + z^2 + R^2 - r^2)^2 = 4 R^2 (x^2 + y^2)\n\nThis equation describes all points (x, y, z) on the torus surface.\n\nThe sphere S with radius 11 centered at the origin has the implicit equation:\n\nx^2 + y^2 + z^2 = 11^2 = 121\n\nTo analyze external tangency, we consider the torus positioned relative to the sphere such that they touch along a circle. The two surfaces are externally tangent along circles, meaning the points of tangency satisfy both surface equations and the gradients of the surfaces are parallel at those points. The tangent circles lie on the torus surface, and their radii correspond to the radius of the circle formed by the intersection of the torus and the sphere at the tangent points. Because the torus is generated by revolving a circle of radius r around an axis at distance R, any circle on the torus parallel to the axis of revolution has radius equal to the distance from the axis minus or plus the minor radius, depending on the position on the torus. The two tangent configurations correspond to the torus touching the sphere externally either on the inner side of the torus tube (closer to the axis) or on the outer side (farther from the axis). Thus, the radii of the tangent circles on the torus are r_i = R - d and r_o = R + d, where d is the distance from the axis to the circle of tangency on the torus tube. Using the tangency condition, the distance from the center of the sphere to the axis of revolution of the torus must be such that the sphere of radius 11 is tangent to the torus tube of radius 3 at these circles. By setting up the distance relations and solving the resulting equations, one finds that the difference r_i - r_o = (R - d) - (R + d) = -2d. The explicit formulas for r_i and r_o in terms of R, r, and the sphere radius S=11 are: r_i = R - sqrt(S^2 - r^2), r_o = R + sqrt(S^2 - r^2). This comes from the fact that the sphere radius squared equals the sum of the square of the minor radius and the square of the distance from the axis to the tangent circle (Pythagorean relation). Therefore, the difference r_i - r_o = (R - sqrt(S^2 - r^2)) - (R + sqrt(S^2 - r^2)) = -2 sqrt(S^2 - r^2). The radius of a circle on the torus at height z is given by the distance from the z-axis to the center of the tube circle at that height, minus or plus the minor radius depending on the position on the tube. The center of the tube circle at height z is at radius R from the z-axis, and the cross-section circle radius is r. The circle of tangency on the torus has radius r_c = sqrt(x^2 + y^2) at height z. Using the sphere equation, z^2 = 121 - r_c^2. The torus equation can be rearranged to relate r_c and z. By applying the tangency condition and solving the system, one finds two solutions for r_c corresponding to the two tangent circles: r_i and r_o. The explicit formulas for these radii are: r_i = R - sqrt((11 - r)^2 - z_i^2) and r_o = R + sqrt((11 + r)^2 - z_o^2), where z_i and z_o are the heights of the tangent circles. More precisely, the two tangent circles correspond to the torus being tangent to the sphere from inside and outside relative to the tube circle. Using the Pythagorean relation and the geometry of the torus and sphere, the radii of the tangent circles on the torus are given by r_i = R - sqrt(11^2 - (r)^2) and r_o = R + sqrt(11^2 - (r)^2). Substituting R=6 and r=3, we get r_i = 6 - sqrt(121 - 9) = 6 - sqrt(112) and r_o = 6 + sqrt(112). import asyncio
from collections import Counter

class LLMAgentBase:
    def __init__(self, output_keys, role, model=None, temperature=0.0, role_name=None):
        self.output_keys = output_keys
        self.role = role
        self.model = model
        self.temperature = temperature
        self.id = id(self)
        self.role_name = role_name
    async def __call__(self, inputs, instruction, round_idx=0, is_sub_task=False):
        # Dummy implementation for testing
        # In real usage, this would call the LLM with inputs and instruction
        thinking = type('obj', (object,), {'content': f"Thinking for: {instruction}"})
        answer = type('obj', (object,), {'content': f"Answer for: {instruction}"})
        return thinking, answer

        print("Step 7: ", sub_tasks[-1])

        # Subtask 8: Evaluate difference r_i - r_o and check rationality (Debate)
        debate_instr_8 = (
            "Sub-task 8: Evaluate the difference r_i - r_o using the derived formulas from subtask_7. "
            "Analyze the expression to determine whether it can be expressed as a rational fraction m/n with relatively prime positive integers. "
            "If the difference contains irrational components, explicitly flag this and avoid unjustified simplifications. "
            "Propose alternative interpretations or request clarification if necessary. "
            "Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
        )
        debate_agents_8 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.0) for role in self.debate_role]
        N_max_8 = self.max_round
        all_thinking8 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_8)]
        all_answer8 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_8)]
        subtask_desc8 = {
            "subtask_id": "subtask_8",
            "instruction": debate_instr_8,
            "context": ["user query", thinking7.content],
            "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
        }
        for r in range(N_max_8):
            for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_8):
                if r == 0:
                    thinking8, answer8 = await agent([taskInfo, thinking7.content], debate_instr_8, r, is_sub_task=True)
                else:
                    input_infos_8 = [taskInfo, thinking7.content] + all_thinking8[r-1]
                    thinking8, answer8 = await agent(input_infos_8, debate_instr_8, r, is_sub_task=True)
                agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, evaluating difference r_i - r_o, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
                all_thinking8[r].append(thinking8)
                all_answer8[r].append(answer8)
        final_decision_agent_8 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
        thinking8, answer8 = await final_decision_agent_8([taskInfo] + all_thinking8[-1], "Sub-task 8: Given all the above thinking and answers, reason over them carefully and provide a final answer.", is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Final Decision agent {final_decision_agent_8.id}, final evaluation of difference r_i - r_o, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
        sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 8 output: thinking - {thinking8.content}; answer - {answer8.content}")
        subtask_desc8['response'] = {"thinking": thinking8, "answer": answer8}
        logs.append(subtask_desc8)
        print("Step 8: ", sub_tasks[-1])

        # Stage 3: Simplify fraction or document impossibility and compute sum m+n

        # Subtask 9: Simplify fraction or document impossibility (SC_CoT)
        cot_sc_instruction_9 = (
            "Sub-task 9: If the difference r_i - r_o is confirmed to be rational, simplify it to lowest terms as a fraction m/n where m and n are relatively prime positive integers. "
            "Otherwise, document the impossibility of expressing the difference as a rational fraction and suggest possible reasons or problem ambiguities."
        )
        cot_agents_9 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0) for _ in range(N)]
        possible_answers_9 = []
        possible_thinkings_9 = []
        subtask_desc9 = {
            "subtask_id": "subtask_9",
            "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_9,
            "context": ["user query", thinking8.content],
            "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
        }
        for i in range(N):
            thinking9, answer9 = await cot_agents_9[i]([taskInfo, thinking8.content], cot_sc_instruction_9, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_9[i].id}, simplifying fraction or documenting impossibility, thinking: {thinking9.content}; answer: {answer9.content}")
            possible_answers_9.append(answer9)
            possible_thinkings_9.append(thinking9)
        final_decision_agent_9 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
        thinking9, answer9 = await final_decision_agent_9([taskInfo] + [t.content for t in possible_thinkings_9], "Sub-task 9: Synthesize and choose the most consistent simplification or documentation.", is_sub_task=True)
        sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 9 output: thinking - {thinking9.content}; answer - {answer9.content}")
        subtask_desc9['response'] = {"thinking": thinking9, "answer": answer9}
        logs.append(subtask_desc9)
        agents.append(f"Final Decision agent {final_decision_agent_9.id}, synthesizing simplification or documentation, thinking: {thinking9.content}; answer: {answer9.content}")
        print("Step 9: ", sub_tasks[-1])

        # Subtask 10: Compute sum m + n and final validation (Reflexion)
        reflect_inst_10 = (
            "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. "
            "Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
        )
        cot_reflect_instruction_10 = (
            "Sub-task 10: Compute the sum m + n from the simplified fraction obtained in subtask_9, ensuring correctness and consistency with the problem statement. "
            "Perform a final validation of all assumptions and results, including the rationality of the answer and the geometric interpretations. "
            + reflect_inst_10
        )
        cot_agent_10 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
        critic_agent_10 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
        N_max_10 = self.max_round
        cot_inputs_10 = [taskInfo, thinking9.content]
        subtask_desc10 = {
            "subtask_id": "subtask_10",
            "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_10,
            "context": ["user query", thinking9.content],
            "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
        }
        thinking10, answer10 = await cot_agent_10(cot_inputs_10, cot_reflect_instruction_10, 0, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_10.id}, final validation, thinking: {thinking10.content}; answer: {answer10.content}")
        for i in range(N_max_10):
            feedback, correct = await critic_agent_10([taskInfo, thinking10.content], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_10.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
            if correct.content.strip() == "True":
                break
            cot_inputs_10.extend([thinking10.content, feedback.content])
            thinking10, answer10 = await cot_agent_10(cot_inputs_10, cot_reflect_instruction_10, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_10.id}, refining final validation, thinking: {thinking10.content}; answer: {answer10.content}")
        sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 10 output: thinking - {thinking10.content}; answer - {answer10.content}")
        subtask_desc10['response'] = {"thinking": thinking10, "answer": answer10}
        logs.append(subtask_desc10)
        print("Step 10: ", sub_tasks[-1])

        final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking10, answer10, sub_tasks, agents)
        return final_answer, logs

async def main():
    workflow = Workflow()
    taskInfo = "Torus T is the surface produced by revolving a circle with radius 3 around an axis in the plane of the circle that is a distance 6 from the center of the circle (so like a donut). Let S be a sphere with a radius 11. When T rests on the outside of S, it is externally tangent to S along a circle with radius r_i, and when T rests on the outside of S, it is externally tangent to S along a circle with radius r_o. The difference r_i-r_o can be written as m/n, where m and n are relatively prime positive integers. Find m+n."
    answer, logs = await workflow.forward(taskInfo)
    print("Final Answer:", answer)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    asyncio.run(main())

============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- A torus T is generated by revolving a circle of radius 3 around an axis in the plane of the circle, with the axis located 6 units from the center of the circle. This creates a standard torus (donut shape) with major radius 6 and minor radius 3.
- A sphere S has radius 11.
- The torus T is placed externally tangent to the sphere S in two different configurations, each time resting on the outside of S.
- In these two configurations, the torus and sphere are tangent along a circle of radius r_i in one case and radius r_o in the other.
- The problem involves the difference r_i - r_o, which can be expressed as a reduced fraction m/n, with m and n positive integers and relatively prime.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The torus is defined by two radii: the major radius (distance from the center of the tube to the center of the torus) R = 6, and the minor radius (radius of the tube) r = 3.
- The sphere has radius 11.
- External tangency along a circle implies that the torus and sphere touch along a common circle, not just a point.
- The two different resting positions of the torus on the sphere correspond to two distinct tangent circles with radii r_i and r_o.
- The difference r_i - r_o relates to geometric properties of the torus-sphere configuration, likely involving distances between centers and radii.
- The problem’s structure depends on understanding how the torus can be positioned relative to the sphere to produce these tangent circles and how their radii relate.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in geometry, specifically 3D geometry involving surfaces of revolution.
- Concepts involved include the geometry of tori and spheres, external tangency conditions, and circle radii on surfaces.
- Subfields include differential geometry (surface properties), classical Euclidean geometry, and possibly analytic geometry if coordinates or equations are used.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and geometric modeling contexts.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The problem states "when T rests on the outside of S" twice, which may be a typographical repetition; presumably, the two tangent configurations differ in orientation or position.
- The exact nature of the two tangent circles (r_i and r_o) and how the torus is positioned in each case is not fully detailed.
- It is not explicitly stated how the torus is oriented relative to the sphere in each tangent configuration.
- Potential challenges include visualizing the 3D arrangement, determining the tangent circles’ radii, and ensuring correct interpretation of "resting on the outside" in both cases.
- The problem assumes familiarity with torus geometry and tangency conditions, which may require careful geometric or algebraic reasoning.

    cot_inputs_2_2 = [taskInfo, thinking_2_1, answer_2_1]

    subtask_2_2_desc = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2_2",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_2_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_2_1.content, answer_2_1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }

    thinking_2_2, answer_2_2 = await cot_agent_2_2(cot_inputs_2_2, cot_reflect_instruction_2_2, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_2.id}, calculating sum m+n, thinking: {thinking_2_2.content}; answer: {answer_2_2.content}")

    for i in range(self.max_round):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_2_2([taskInfo, thinking_2_2], "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_2_2.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_2_2.extend([thinking_2_2, feedback])
        thinking_2_2, answer_2_2 = await cot_agent_2_2(cot_inputs_2_2, cot_reflect_instruction_2_2, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_2.id}, refining sum calculation, thinking: {thinking_2_2.content}; answer: {answer_2_2.content}")

    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2_2 output: thinking - {thinking_2_2.content}; answer - {answer_2_2.content}")
    subtask_2_2_desc["response"] = {"thinking": thinking_2_2, "answer": answer_2_2}
    logs.append(subtask_2_2_desc)
    print("Step 2_2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking_2_2, answer_2_2, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

    print("Step 1_2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Stage 2: Compute difference and final sum

    # Subtask 2_1: Compute difference r_i - r_o and simplify fraction (Reflexion)
    reflect_inst_2_1 = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction_2_1 = (
        "Sub-task 2_1: Compute the difference r_i - r_o using the validated expressions and numeric values. "
        "Simplify the result into a reduced fraction m/n where m and n are positive integers with no common factors. "
        "Cross-validate the arithmetic simplification against the numeric approximations to prevent transcription or simplification errors. "
        "Document the simplification steps clearly. " + reflect_inst_2_1
    )
    cot_agent_2_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_2_1 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_2_1 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_2_1 = [taskInfo, thinking_1_2.content, answer_1_2.content]
    subtask_desc_2_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2_1",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_2_1,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_1_2.content, answer_1_2.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking_2_1, answer_2_1 = await cot_agent_2_1(cot_inputs_2_1, cot_reflect_instruction_2_1, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_1.id}, compute and simplify difference r_i - r_o, thinking: {thinking_2_1.content}; answer: {answer_2_1.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_2_1):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_2_1([taskInfo, thinking_2_1.content], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_2_1.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_2_1.extend([thinking_2_1, feedback.content])
        thinking_2_1, answer_2_1 = await cot_agent_2_1(cot_inputs_2_1, cot_reflect_instruction_2_1, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_1.id}, refining difference computation, thinking: {thinking_2_1.content}; answer: {answer_2_1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2_1 output: thinking - {thinking_2_1.content}; answer - {answer_2_1.content}")
    subtask_desc_2_1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_2_1, "answer": answer_2_1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_2_1)
    print("Step 2_1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Subtask 2_2: Calculate sum m + n (Reflexion)
    reflect_inst_2_2 = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction_2_2 = (
        "Sub-task 2_2: Calculate the sum m + n from the simplified fraction obtained for r_i - r_o. "
        "Confirm that this final answer matches the problem requirements and is consistent with all previous numeric and algebraic results. "
        "Prepare the final output ensuring clarity and correctness. " + reflect_inst_2_2
    )
    cot_agent_2_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_2_2 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_2_2 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_2_2 = [taskInfo, thinking_2_1.content, answer_2_1.content]
    subtask_desc_2_2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2_2",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_2_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_2_1.content, answer_2_1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking_2_2, answer_2_2 = await cot_agent_2_2(cot_inputs_2_2, cot_reflect_instruction_2_2, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_2.id}, calculate sum m + n, thinking: {thinking_2_2.content}; answer: {answer_2_2.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_2_2):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_2_2([taskInfo, thinking_2_2.content], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_2_2.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_2_2.extend([thinking_2_2, feedback.content])
        thinking_2_2, answer_2_2 = await cot_agent_2_2(cot_inputs_2_2, cot_reflect_instruction_2_2, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_2.id}, refining sum calculation, thinking: {thinking_2_2.content}; answer: {answer_2_2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2_2 output: thinking - {thinking_2_2.content}; answer - {answer_2_2.content}")
    subtask_desc_2_2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_2_2, "answer": answer_2_2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_2_2)
    print("Step 2_2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Subtask 2_3: Final consistency check (Debate)
    debate_instruction_2_3 = (
        "Sub-task 2_3: Perform a final consistency check reviewing all numeric results, algebraic formulas, and arithmetic simplifications. "
        "Verify that all values satisfy the geometric and arithmetic constraints of the problem. Confirm that the fraction m/n is in lowest terms and that the final sum m + n is correct. "
        "Address any inconsistencies before finalizing the answer. "
        "Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
    )
    debate_agents_2_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.0) for role in self.debate_role]
    N_max_2_3 = self.max_round
    all_thinking_2_3 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_2_3)]
    all_answer_2_3 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_2_3)]
    subtask_desc_2_3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2_3",
        "instruction": debate_instruction_2_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_2_2.content, answer_2_2.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }
    for r in range(N_max_2_3):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_2_3):
            if r == 0:
                thinking, answer = await agent([taskInfo, thinking_2_2.content, answer_2_2.content], debate_instruction_2_3, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos = [taskInfo, thinking_2_2.content, answer_2_2.content] + all_thinking_2_3[r-1]
                thinking, answer = await agent(input_infos, debate_instruction_2_3, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, final consistency check, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
            all_thinking_2_3[r].append(thinking)
            all_answer_2_3[r].append(answer)
    final_decision_agent_2_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking_2_3, answer_2_3 = await final_decision_agent_2_3([taskInfo] + all_thinking_2_3[-1], "Sub-task 2_3: Synthesize and finalize consistency check.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2_3 output: thinking - {thinking_2_3.content}; answer - {answer_2_3.content}")
    subtask_desc_2_3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_2_3, "answer": answer_2_3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_2_3)
    print("Step 2_3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking_2_3, answer_2_3, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs
